<script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    var allowedURLs = ['https://cvclavoz.com/afiliadas/'];
    var currentURL = window.location.href;
    var isAllowedURL = allowedURLs.some(function (allowedURL) {
        return currentURL.includes(allowedURL);
    });

    if (isAllowedURL) {
        var buttonsNext = document.querySelectorAll('.elementor-button.elementor-size-sm e-form__buttons__wrapper__button.e-form__buttons__wrapper__button-next');
        var buttonsPrev = document.querySelectorAll('.e-form__buttons__wrapper__button-previous');
        var sendButton = document.getElementById('send-afilidas');

        console.log('Next button ready', buttonsNext);
        console.log('Send button ready', sendButton);

        function handleNextButtonClick() {
            var activeIndicator = document.querySelector('.e-form__indicators__indicator--state-active .e-form__indicators__indicator__number');
            var activeIndicatorText = activeIndicator ? activeIndicator.textContent : '';

            console.log('Next button clicked');
            console.log('Active Indicator:', activeIndicatorText);

            window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
            window.dataLayer.push({
                'event': 'cv_select_form_afiliadas_next',
                'element_name': 'Select form next',
                'indicator_state_active': activeIndicatorText
            });
        }

        function handlePrevButtonClick() {
            var activeIndicator = document.querySelector('.e-form__indicators__indicator--state-active .e-form__indicators__indicator__number');
            var activeIndicatorText = activeIndicator ? activeIndicator.textContent : '';

            console.log('Previous button clicked');
            console.log('Active Indicator:', activeIndicatorText);

            window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
            window.dataLayer.push({
                'event': 'cv_select_form_afiliadas_prev',
                'element_name': 'Select form previous',
                'indicator_state_active': activeIndicatorText
            });
        }

        function handleSendButtonClick() {
            console.log('Send button clicked');

            window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
            window.dataLayer.push({
                'event': 'cv_select_form_afiliadas',
                'element_name': 'Select afiliadas form'
            });
        }
		
		buttonsNext.forEach(function(button) {
            button.addEventListener('click', handleNextButtonClick);
        });

        buttonsPrev.forEach(function(button) {
            button.addEventListener('click', handlePrevButtonClick);
        });

        if (sendButton) {
            sendButton.addEventListener('click', handleSendButtonClick);
        }
    }
});

</script>
<!-- Botones Academia -->
<script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    var allowedURLs = [
        'https://cvclavoz.com/academia/'
    ];

    var currentURL = window.location.href;
    var isAllowedURL = allowedURLs.some(function (allowedURL) {
        return currentURL.includes(allowedURL);
    });

    function handleCLickEvent(year) {
        return function(event) {
            var labelElement = this.querySelector('.elementor-button-content-wrapper');
            var elementText = labelElement.innerText;
            window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
            window.dataLayer.push({
                'event': 'cv_academia_year',
                'element_name': `Academia - ${year}`
            });
        };
    }

    if (isAllowedURL) {
        var parentContainer2022 = document.getElementById('academia_2022');
        var parentContainer2023 = document.getElementById('academia_2023');

        if (parentContainer2022 || parentContainer2023) {
            var childElement2022 = parentContainer2022.querySelector('.elementor-button.elementor-button-link.elementor-size-sm');
            var childElement2023 = parentContainer2023.querySelector('.elementor-button.elementor-button-link.elementor-size-sm');

            if (childElement2022 && childElement2023) { 
                var year2022 = 2022;
                var year2023 = 2023;
                childElement2022.addEventListener('click', handleCLickEvent(year2022));
                childElement2023.addEventListener('click', handleCLickEvent(year2023));
            }
        }
    }
});
</script>

                    'event': 'newsletter',

            });

<script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
	document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
  // Verificar si la URL actual está en la lista de URLs permitidas
  var allowedURLs = [
    'https://cvclavoz.com/blog/',
    'https://cvclavoz.com/blog/recursos-para-iglesias/',
    'https/cvclavoz.com/blog/familia/',
    'https://cvclavoz.com/blog/estilo-de-vida-bienestar/',
    'https://cvclavoz.com/blog/amor-y-pareja/',
    'https://cvclavoz.com/blog/inspiracional/',
    'https://cvclavoz.com/blog/preguntas-y-respuestas/',
    'https://cvclavoz.com/te-ayudamos/',
    'https://cvclavoz.com/te-ayudamos/devocionales/',
    'https://cvclavoz.com/te-ayudamos/oracion/',
    'https://cvclavoz.com/te-ayudamos/versiculos/'
  ];

    var currentURL = window.location.href;
    var isAllowedURL = allowedURLs.some(function (allowedURL) {
        return currentURL.includes(allowedURL);
    });
  if (isAllowedURL) {
    // Función para enviar el dataLayer
    function sendDataLayer(elementName, elementText) {
	  var labelElement = document.querySelector('.elementor-share-btn__title');
      var elementosArticulo = labelElement.innerText;
      window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
      window.dataLayer.push({
        'event': 'cv_redes_sociales_post',
        'element_name': `${elementName}`,
        'element_text': elementText
      });
    }

    // Selector para los botones de redes sociales
    var socialMediaClasses = ['elementor-share-btn_facebook', 'elementor-share-btn_twitter', 'elementor-share-btn_email', 'elementor-share-btn_linkedin', 'elementor-share-btn_whatsapp'];

    socialMediaClasses.forEach(function (socialMediaClass) {
      var buttons = document.querySelectorAll('#social-media .' + socialMediaClass);

      buttons.forEach(function (button) {
        var elementName;

        // Determina el nombre del botón clicado
        switch (socialMediaClass) {
          case 'elementor-share-btn_facebook':
            elementName = 'Facebook';
            break;
          case 'elementor-share-btn_twitter':
            elementName = 'Twitter';
            break;
          case 'elementor-share-btn_email':
            elementName = 'Email';
            break;
          case 'elementor-share-btn_linkedin':
            elementName = 'LinkedIn';
            break;
          case 'elementor-share-btn_whatsapp':
            elementName = 'Whatsapp';
            break;
          default:
            elementName = 'Red Social Desconocida';
        }

        button.id = "red_social_post";
        button.addEventListener('click', function () {
		  
          var elementosArticulos = document.querySelectorAll('.title_article');
          var nombreDelArticulo = elementosArticulos[0].innerText; // Obtén el texto del artículo
		  console.log("Click")	
		  console.log("elementName", elementName)
		  console.log("nombreDelArticulo",nombreDelArticulo)

          // Envía el DataLayer
          sendDataLayer(elementName, nombreDelArticulo);
        });
      });
    });
  }
});

</script>

<!-- Boton guardar y eliminar en blog y Te Ayudamos -->
<script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    var allowedURLs = [
        'https://cvclavoz.com/blog/',
        'https://cvclavoz.com/blog/recursos-para-iglesias/',
        'https://cvclavoz.com/blog/familia/',
        'https://cvclavoz.com/blog/estilo-de-vida-bienestar/',
        'https://cvclavoz.com/blog/amor-y-pareja/',
        'https://cvclavoz.com/blog/inspiracional/',
        'https://cvclavoz.com/blog/preguntas-y-respuestas/',
        'https://cvclavoz.com/te-ayudamos/',
        'https://cvclavoz.com/te-ayudamos/devocionales/',
        'https://cvclavoz.com/te-ayudamos/oracion/',
        'https://cvclavoz.com/te-ayudamos/versiculos/'
    ];

    var currentURL = window.location.href;

    var isAllowedURL = allowedURLs.some(function (allowedURL) {
        return currentURL.includes(allowedURL);
    });

    function handleCLickEvent(event) {
		var tituloDelArticulo = document.querySelector('.title_article h1').innerText; 
        // Extraer el texto de jet-listing-dynamic-link__label
        var labelElement = this.querySelector('.jet-listing-dynamic-link__label');
        var elementosArticulo = labelElement.innerText;

        // Determinar si es para "Guardar" o "Eliminar"
        var elementAction = elementosArticulo.includes('Guardar Post') ? 'Guardar' : 'Eliminar';

        // Crear y enviar el evento dataLayer
        window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
        window.dataLayer.push({
            'event': 'cv_guardar_post',
            'element_name': `${elementAction} artículo`,
            'element_text': `${tituloDelArticulo}`
        });
    }

    if (isAllowedURL) {
        var dynamicLinkElement = document.querySelector('#guardar_post .elementor-widget-container .jet-listing-dynamic-link');
        
        if (dynamicLinkElement) {
            dynamicLinkElement.addEventListener('click', handleCLickEvent);
        } 
    }
});

</script>

<!-- Podcast mas escuchados -->
<script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        var allowedURLs = [
            'https://cvclavoz.com/podcasts-cvclavoz/'
        ];

        var currentURL = window.location.href;

        if (allowedURLs.includes(currentURL)) {
            var botones = document.querySelectorAll('.me-3.play_btn__playButton___yPmEJ');
            var elementosArticulosNodeList = document.querySelectorAll('.style__item___ILRsH');

            // Usar un Set para almacenar elementos únicos
            var elementosArticulosSet = new Set();

            // Agregar elementos al Set
            elementosArticulosNodeList.forEach(function(elementoArticulo) {
                elementosArticulosSet.add(elementoArticulo.textContent.trim());
            });

            // Convertir el Set en un array
            var elementosArticulos = Array.from(elementosArticulosSet);

            for (var i = 0; i < botones.length; i++) {
                var boton = botones[i];
                var elementoArticulo = elementosArticulos[i];

                if (boton && elementoArticulo) {
                    boton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                        // Obtiene el nombre del podcast
                        var nombreDelPodcast = elementoArticulo;
                        // Crea y envía el evento dataLayer
                        window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
                        window.dataLayer.push({
                            'event': 'cv_select_podcast_most_view',
                            'element_name': 'Seleccionar podcast',
                            'element_text': nombreDelPodcast
                        });
                    });
                }
            }
        }
    });
</script>

<!-- Articulos blog y Te Ayudamos -->
<script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        var allowedURLs = [
            'https://cvclavoz.com/',
            'https://cvclavoz.com/blog/',
            'https://cvclavoz.com/blog/recursos-para-iglesias/',
            'https://cvclavoz.com/blog/familia/',
            'https://cvclavoz.com/blog/estilo-de-vida-bienestar/',
            'https://cvclavoz.com/blog/amor-y-pareja/',
            'https://cvclavoz.com/blog/inspiracional/',
            'https://cvclavoz.com/blog/preguntas-y-respuestas/',
            'https://cvclavoz.com/te-ayudamos/',
            'https://cvclavoz.com/te-ayudamos/devocionales/',
            'https://cvclavoz.com/te-ayudamos/oracion/',
            'https://cvclavoz.com/te-ayudamos/versiculos/'
        ];

        var currentURL = window.location.href;

        if (allowedURLs.includes(currentURL)) {
            function setupEventListener() {
                // Código JavaScript aquí
                var botones = document.querySelectorAll('.haz_click_ahora_articles');
                var elementosArticulos = document.querySelectorAll('.title_select_articles');

                for (var i = 0; i < botones.length; i++) {
                    var boton = botones[i];
                    var elementoArticulo = elementosArticulos[i];

                    if (boton && elementoArticulo) {
                        boton.addEventListener('click', function (articulo) {
                            return function () {
                                // Obtiene el nombre del artículo
                                var nombreDelArticulo = articulo.textContent.trim();
                                // Crea y envía la capa de datos
                                window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
                                window.dataLayer.push({
                                    'event': 'cv_select_articles',
                                    'element_name': 'Seleccionar artículo',
                                    'element_text': nombreDelArticulo
                                });
                            };
                        }(elementoArticulo));
                    }
                }
            }

            function reiniciarDOM() {
                // Vuelve a renderizar los elementos .haz_click_ahora_articles
                setupEventListener();
            }

            document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', reiniciarDOM);

            function agregarEventos() {
                var cargarBotones = document.querySelectorAll('.cargar-mas-selector');
                if (cargarBotones) {
                    cargarBotones.forEach(function (cargarBoton) {
                        cargarBoton.addEventListener('click', reiniciarDOM);
                    });
                }
            }

            // Escucha el evento 'load' para asegurarse de que todos los recursos se hayan cargado
            window.addEventListener('load', agregarEventos);
        }
    });
</script>

<!-- haz_clic_ahora = categorias Te ayudamos-->
<script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        // Verifica la URL actual
        var currentURL = window.location.href;
        var allowedURLs = [
            'https://cvclavoz.com/te-ayudamos/',
            'https://cvclavoz.com/te-ayudamos/devocionales/',
            'https://cvclavoz.com/te-ayudamos/oracion/',
            'https://cvclavoz.com/te-ayudamos/versiculos/'
        ];

        if (allowedURLs.includes(currentURL)) {
		
            var botones = document.querySelectorAll('.haz_clic_ahora');
            var elementosCategoria = {};

            // Asigna los elementos correspondientes a cada tipo de ID
            var tiposDeID = ['devocionales', 'oracion', 'versiculos'];

            for (var i = 0; i < tiposDeID.length; i++) {
                var tipoID = tiposDeID[i];
                elementosCategoria[tipoID] = document.getElementById('title_select_te_ayudamos_' + tipoID);

                if (elementosCategoria[tipoID]) {
                    botones[i].addEventListener('click', (function (categoria) {
                        return function () {
                            // Obtiene el nombre de la categoría
                            var nombreDeCategoria = categoria.textContent.trim();
                            // Crear y enviar la capa de datos
                            window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
                            window.dataLayer.push({
                                'event': 'cv_select_categories',
                                'element_name': 'Seleccionar categoría',
                                'element_text': nombreDeCategoria
                            });
                        };
                    })(elementosCategoria[tipoID]));
                }
            }
        }
    });
</script>

<!--WhatsApp Chat Widget Start-->
<script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
    // Create a div container with an id
    const whatsappContainer = document.createElement("div");
    whatsappContainer.id = "whatsapp-container";

    // Create a WhatsApp link
    const whatsappLink = document.createElement("a");
    whatsappLink.href = "https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VaDb27Y8KMqoBDKyFJ0s";
    whatsappLink.target = "_blank";

    // Create an image element for the WhatsApp icon
    const whatsappIcon = document.createElement("img");
    whatsappIcon.src =
      "https://cvclavoz.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/logo-whatsapp.png";
    whatsappIcon.alt = "WhatsApp";

    // Add a tooltip (message on hover)
    whatsappLink.title = "Contáctanos por WhatsApp";

    // Append the WhatsApp icon to the link
    whatsappLink.appendChild(whatsappIcon);

    // Apply CSS styles to the container
    whatsappContainer.style.position = "fixed";
    whatsappContainer.style.zIndex = "1000";
    whatsappContainer.style.right = "20px";
    whatsappContainer.style.bottom = "20px";

    // Apply CSS styles to the icon
    whatsappIcon.style.width = "60px";
    whatsappIcon.style.height = "60px";

    // Adjust the size and position based on screen width
    const updateStylesForScreen = () => {
      if (window.innerWidth <= 768) {
        // For mobile screens
        whatsappIcon.style.width = "50px";
        whatsappIcon.style.height = "50px";
      } else if (window.innerWidth <= 1024) {
        // For tablets
        whatsappIcon.style.width = "55px";
        whatsappIcon.style.height = "55px";
      } else {
        // For desktop screens
        whatsappIcon.style.width = "60px";
        whatsappIcon.style.height = "60px";
      }
    };

    // Initial update
    updateStylesForScreen();

    // Update styles on window resize
    window.addEventListener("resize", updateStylesForScreen);

    // Add the WhatsApp link to the container
    whatsappContainer.appendChild(whatsappLink);

    // Add the container to the document body
    document.body.appendChild(whatsappContainer);
  });
</script>
<!--WhatsApp Chat Widget End-->


<!--Spotify Chat Widget in Podcasts Start-->
<script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
    if (window.location.href === 'https://cvclavoz.com/podcasts-cvclavoz/') {
      // Create a div container with an id
      const spotifyContainer = document.createElement('div');
      spotifyContainer.id = 'spotify-container';

      // Create a Spotify link
      const spotifyLink = document.createElement('a');
      spotifyLink.href = 'https://open.spotify.com/search/cvclavoz';
      spotifyLink.target = '_blank';

      // Create an image element for the Spotify icon
      const spotifyIcon = document.createElement('img');
      spotifyIcon.src = 'https://cvclavoz.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/spotify-logo-png-7053.png';
      spotifyIcon.alt = 'Spotify';

      // Apply CSS styles to set the size
      spotifyIcon.style.width = '60px';
      spotifyIcon.style.height = '60px';

      // Add a tooltip (message on hover)
      spotifyLink.title = 'Escúchanos en Spotify';

      // Append the Spotify icon to the link
      spotifyLink.appendChild(spotifyIcon);

      // Apply CSS styles to the container
      spotifyContainer.style.position = 'fixed';
      spotifyContainer.style.zIndex = '1000';
      spotifyContainer.style.right = '20px';

      // Adjust the position above the WhatsApp widget
      const updateSpotifyPosition = () => {
        if (window.innerWidth <= 768) {
          // For mobile screens
          spotifyContainer.style.bottom = '135px'; // Above WhatsApp
          spotifyIcon.style.width = '50px';
          spotifyIcon.style.height = '50px';
        } else if (window.innerWidth <= 1024) {
          // For tablets
          spotifyContainer.style.bottom = '130px'; // Above WhatsApp
          spotifyIcon.style.width = '55px';
          spotifyIcon.style.height = '55px';
        } else {
          // For desktop screens
          spotifyContainer.style.bottom = '100px'; // Above WhatsApp
          spotifyIcon.style.width = '60px';
          spotifyIcon.style.height = '60px';
        }
      };

      // Initial update
      updateSpotifyPosition();

      // Update styles on window resize
      window.addEventListener("resize", updateSpotifyPosition);

      // Add the Spotify link to the container
      spotifyContainer.appendChild(spotifyLink);

      // Add the container to the document body
      document.body.appendChild(spotifyContainer);
    }
  });
</script>
<!--Spotify Chat Widget in Podcasts End-->

<script type="rocketlazyloadscript" data-rocket-type="text/javascript">(function (undefined) {let scriptOptions={"_localizedStrings":{"redirect_overlay_title":"Espera","redirect_overlay_text":"Est\u00e1s siendo redirigido a otra p\u00e1gina,<br>puede tardar unos segundos.","webview_notification_text":"The selected provider doesn't support embedded browsers!"},"_targetWindow":"prefer-popup","_redirectOverlay":"overlay-with-spinner-and-message","_unsupportedWebviewBehavior":""};
/**
 * Used when Cross-Origin-Opener-Policy blocked the access to the opener. We can't have a reference of the opened windows, so we should attempt to refresh only the windows that has opened popups.
 */
window._nslHasOpenedPopup = false;
window._nslWebViewNoticeElement = null;

window.NSLPopup = function (url, title, w, h) {

    /**
     * Cross-Origin-Opener-Policy blocked the access to the opener
     */
    if (typeof BroadcastChannel === "function") {
        const _nslLoginBroadCastChannel = new BroadcastChannel('nsl_login_broadcast_channel');
        _nslLoginBroadCastChannel.onmessage = (event) => {
            if (window?._nslHasOpenedPopup && event.data?.action === 'redirect') {
                window._nslHasOpenedPopup = false;

                const url = event.data?.href;
                _nslLoginBroadCastChannel.close();
                if (typeof window.nslRedirect === 'function') {
                    window.nslRedirect(url);
                } else {
                    window.opener.location = url;
                }
            }
        };
    }

    const userAgent = navigator.userAgent,
        mobile = function () {
            return /\b(iPhone|iP[ao]d)/.test(userAgent) ||
                /\b(iP[ao]d)/.test(userAgent) ||
                /Android/i.test(userAgent) ||
                /Mobile/i.test(userAgent);
        },
        screenX = window.screenX !== undefined ? window.screenX : window.screenLeft,
        screenY = window.screenY !== undefined ? window.screenY : window.screenTop,
        outerWidth = window.outerWidth !== undefined ? window.outerWidth : document.documentElement.clientWidth,
        outerHeight = window.outerHeight !== undefined ? window.outerHeight : document.documentElement.clientHeight - 22,
        targetWidth = mobile() ? null : w,
        targetHeight = mobile() ? null : h,
        left = parseInt(screenX + (outerWidth - targetWidth) / 2, 10),
        right = parseInt(screenY + (outerHeight - targetHeight) / 2.5, 10),
        features = [];
    if (targetWidth !== null) {
        features.push('width=' + targetWidth);
    }
    if (targetHeight !== null) {
        features.push('height=' + targetHeight);
    }
    features.push('left=' + left);
    features.push('top=' + right);
    features.push('scrollbars=1');

    const newWindow = window.open(url, title, features.join(','));

    if (window.focus) {
        newWindow.focus();
    }

    window._nslHasOpenedPopup = true;

    return newWindow;
};

let isWebView = null;

function checkWebView() {
    if (isWebView === null) {
        function _detectOS(ua) {
            if (/Android/.test(ua)) {
                return "Android";
            } else if (/iPhone|iPad|iPod/.test(ua)) {
                return "iOS";
            } else if (/Windows/.test(ua)) {
                return "Windows";
            } else if (/Mac OS X/.test(ua)) {
                return "Mac";
            } else if (/CrOS/.test(ua)) {
                return "Chrome OS";
            } else if (/Firefox/.test(ua)) {
                return "Firefox OS";
            }
            return "";
        }

        function _detectBrowser(ua) {
            let android = /Android/.test(ua);

            if (/Opera Mini/.test(ua) || / OPR/.test(ua) || / OPT/.test(ua)) {
                return "Opera";
            } else if (/CriOS/.test(ua)) {
                return "Chrome for iOS";
            } else if (/Edge/.test(ua)) {
                return "Edge";
            } else if (android && /Silk\//.test(ua)) {
                return "Silk";
            } else if (/Chrome/.test(ua)) {
                return "Chrome";
            } else if (/Firefox/.test(ua)) {
                return "Firefox";
            } else if (android) {
                return "AOSP";
            } else if (/MSIE|Trident/.test(ua)) {
                return "IE";
            } else if (/Safari\//.test(ua)) {
                return "Safari";
            } else if (/AppleWebKit/.test(ua)) {
                return "WebKit";
            }
            return "";
        }

        function _detectBrowserVersion(ua, browser) {
            if (browser === "Opera") {
                return /Opera Mini/.test(ua) ? _getVersion(ua, "Opera Mini/") :
                    / OPR/.test(ua) ? _getVersion(ua, " OPR/") :
                        _getVersion(ua, " OPT/");
            } else if (browser === "Chrome for iOS") {
                return _getVersion(ua, "CriOS/");
            } else if (browser === "Edge") {
                return _getVersion(ua, "Edge/");
            } else if (browser === "Chrome") {
                return _getVersion(ua, "Chrome/");
            } else if (browser === "Firefox") {
                return _getVersion(ua, "Firefox/");
            } else if (browser === "Silk") {
                return _getVersion(ua, "Silk/");
            } else if (browser === "AOSP") {
                return _getVersion(ua, "Version/");
            } else if (browser === "IE") {
                return /IEMobile/.test(ua) ? _getVersion(ua, "IEMobile/") :
                    /MSIE/.test(ua) ? _getVersion(ua, "MSIE ")
                        :
                        _getVersion(ua, "rv:");
            } else if (browser === "Safari") {
                return _getVersion(ua, "Version/");
            } else if (browser === "WebKit") {
                return _getVersion(ua, "WebKit/");
            }
            return "0.0.0";
        }

        function _getVersion(ua, token) {
            try {
                return _normalizeSemverString(ua.split(token)[1].trim().split(/[^\w\.]/)[0]);
            } catch (o_O) {
            }
            return "0.0.0";
        }

        function _normalizeSemverString(version) {
            const ary = version.split(/[\._]/);
            return (parseInt(ary[0], 10) || 0) + "." +
                (parseInt(ary[1], 10) || 0) + "." +
                (parseInt(ary[2], 10) || 0);
        }

        function _isWebView(ua, os, browser, version, options) {
            switch (os + browser) {
                case "iOSSafari":
                    return false;
                case "iOSWebKit":
                    return _isWebView_iOS(options);
                case "AndroidAOSP":
                    return false;
                case "AndroidChrome":
                    return parseFloat(version) >= 42 ? /; wv/.test(ua) : /\d{2}\.0\.0/.test(version) ? true : _isWebView_Android(options);
            }
            return false;
        }

        function _isWebView_iOS(options) {
            const document = (window["document"] || {});

            if ("WEB_VIEW" in options) {
                return options["WEB_VIEW"];
            }
            return !("fullscreenEnabled" in document || "webkitFullscreenEnabled" in document || false);
        }

        function _isWebView_Android(options) {
            if ("WEB_VIEW" in options) {
                return options["WEB_VIEW"];
            }
            return !("requestFileSystem" in window || "webkitRequestFileSystem" in window || false);
        }

        const options = {},
            nav = window.navigator || {},
            ua = nav.userAgent || "",
            os = _detectOS(ua),
            browser = _detectBrowser(ua),
            browserVersion = _detectBrowserVersion(ua, browser);

        isWebView = _isWebView(ua, os, browser, browserVersion, options);
    }

    return isWebView;
}

function isAllowedWebViewForUserAgent(provider) {
    const facebookAllowedWebViews = [
        'Instagram',
        'FBAV',
        'FBAN'
    ];
    let whitelist = [];

    if (provider && provider === 'facebook') {
        whitelist = facebookAllowedWebViews;
    }

    const nav = window.navigator || {},
        ua = nav.userAgent || "";

    if (whitelist.length && ua.match(new RegExp(whitelist.join('|')))) {
        return true;
    }

    return false;
}

function disableButtonInWebView(providerButtonElement) {
    if (providerButtonElement) {
        providerButtonElement.classList.add('nsl-disabled-provider');
        providerButtonElement.setAttribute('href', '#');

        providerButtonElement.addEventListener('pointerdown', (e) => {
            if (!window._nslWebViewNoticeElement) {
                window._nslWebViewNoticeElement = document.createElement('div');
                window._nslWebViewNoticeElement.id = "nsl-notices-fallback";
                window._nslWebViewNoticeElement.addEventListener('pointerdown', function (e) {
                    this.parentNode.removeChild(this);
                    window._nslWebViewNoticeElement = null;
                });
                const webviewNoticeHTML = '<div class="error"><p>' + scriptOptions._localizedStrings.webview_notification_text + '</p></div>';

                window._nslWebViewNoticeElement.insertAdjacentHTML("afterbegin", webviewNoticeHTML);
                document.body.appendChild(window._nslWebViewNoticeElement);
            }
        });
    }

}

window._nslDOMReady(function () {

    window.nslRedirect = function (url) {
        if (scriptOptions._redirectOverlay) {
            const overlay = document.createElement('div');
            overlay.id = "nsl-redirect-overlay";
            let overlayHTML = '';
            const overlayContainer = "<div id='nsl-redirect-overlay-container'>",
                overlayContainerClose = "</div>",
                overlaySpinner = "<div id='nsl-redirect-overlay-spinner'></div>",
                overlayTitle = "<p id='nsl-redirect-overlay-title'>" + scriptOptions._localizedStrings.redirect_overlay_title + "</p>",
                overlayText = "<p id='nsl-redirect-overlay-text'>" + scriptOptions._localizedStrings.redirect_overlay_text + "</p>";

            switch (scriptOptions._redirectOverlay) {
                case "overlay-only":
                    break;
                case "overlay-with-spinner":
                    overlayHTML = overlayContainer + overlaySpinner + overlayContainerClose;
                    break;
                default:
                    overlayHTML = overlayContainer + overlaySpinner + overlayTitle + overlayText + overlayContainerClose;
                    break;
            }

            overlay.insertAdjacentHTML("afterbegin", overlayHTML);
            document.body.appendChild(overlay);
        }

        window.location = url;
    };

    let targetWindow = scriptOptions._targetWindow || 'prefer-popup',
        lastPopup = false;


    document.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
        if (e.target) {
            const buttonLinkElement = e.target.closest('a[data-plugin="nsl"][data-action="connect"]') || e.target.closest('a[data-plugin="nsl"][data-action="link"]');
            if (buttonLinkElement) {
                if (lastPopup && !lastPopup.closed) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    lastPopup.focus();
                } else {

                    let href = buttonLinkElement.href,
                        success = false;
                    if (href.indexOf('?') !== -1) {
                        href += '&';
                    } else {
                        href += '?';
                    }

                    const redirectTo = buttonLinkElement.dataset.redirect;
                    if (redirectTo === 'current') {
                        href += 'redirect=' + encodeURIComponent(window.location.href) + '&';
                    } else if (redirectTo && redirectTo !== '') {
                        href += 'redirect=' + encodeURIComponent(redirectTo) + '&';
                    }

                    if (targetWindow !== 'prefer-same-window' && checkWebView()) {
                        targetWindow = 'prefer-same-window';
                    }

                    if (targetWindow === 'prefer-popup') {
                        lastPopup = NSLPopup(href + 'display=popup', 'nsl-social-connect', buttonLinkElement.dataset.popupwidth, buttonLinkElement.dataset.popupheight);
                        if (lastPopup) {
                            success = true;
                            e.preventDefault();
                        }
                    } else if (targetWindow === 'prefer-new-tab') {
                        const newTab = window.open(href + 'display=popup', '_blank');
                        if (newTab) {
                            if (window.focus) {
                                newTab.focus();
                            }
                            success = true;
                            window._nslHasOpenedPopup = true;
                            e.preventDefault();
                        }
                    }

                    if (!success) {
                        window.location = href;
                        e.preventDefault();
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    });

    let buttonCountChanged = false;

    const googleLoginButtons = document.querySelectorAll(' a[data-plugin="nsl"][data-provider="google"]');
    if (googleLoginButtons.length && checkWebView()) {
        googleLoginButtons.forEach(function (googleLoginButton) {
            if (scriptOptions._unsupportedWebviewBehavior === 'disable-button') {
                disableButtonInWebView(googleLoginButton);
            } else {
                googleLoginButton.remove();
                buttonCountChanged = true;
            }
        });
    }

    const facebookLoginButtons = document.querySelectorAll(' a[data-plugin="nsl"][data-provider="facebook"]');
    if (facebookLoginButtons.length && checkWebView() && /Android/.test(window.navigator.userAgent) && !isAllowedWebViewForUserAgent('facebook')) {
        facebookLoginButtons.forEach(function (facebookLoginButton) {
            if (scriptOptions._unsupportedWebviewBehavior === 'disable-button') {
                disableButtonInWebView(facebookLoginButton);
            } else {
                facebookLoginButton.remove();
                buttonCountChanged = true;
            }
        });
    }

    const separators = document.querySelectorAll('div.nsl-separator');
    if (buttonCountChanged && separators.length) {
        separators.forEach(function (separator) {
            const separatorParentNode = separator.parentNode;
            if (separatorParentNode) {
                const separatorButtonContainer = separatorParentNode.querySelector('div.nsl-container-buttons');
                if (separatorButtonContainer && !separatorButtonContainer.hasChildNodes()) {
                    separator.remove();
                }
            }
        })
    }
});})();</script>
